yet another movie about the difficulties of movie making. the film industry has a narcissistic complex. grow up, if movie making is so difficult, go to the fields and grow some crops (as the trailer correctly points out). no one cares if a movie is made or not, but if there is no food on the table everyone is concerned. my advice to the movie industry is to focus on stuff that is really difficult, and yet is not entertainment - like trying to open a factory in the midst of militant labour unionism for example. and yes, i include sports in entertainment. such movies will be socially relevant and also provide some motivation to the many youth who are desperate to leave kerala thanks to the destructive politics that makes life of an entrepreneur hell.

After watching this trailer I think Vineeth Sreenivasan is taking a sweet revenge from what Mohanlal did to Sreenivasan.  This film seems more of a role reversal where instead of Mohanlal/Pranav playing the good guys what we have witnessed for more than 3 decades in the Malayalam film industry now we set to see Sreenivasan/Dhyaan/Vineeth playing the good cop.  I understand your feeling Vineeth Sreenivasan your father must be very proud of this film.  This movie will be special for both Mohanlal and Sreenivasan they sure will feel a gush of emotions while watching the film.
